Source Code

These source-code files are part of a reconstructed copy of Artemis 071, the first release of the Apollo 15 through 17 Command Module (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) software.

The reconstruction began with source code of Artemis 072 previously transcribed from a digitized copy of that program. The code was then updated by undoing changes between the two versions. The reconstruction was verified by matching memory-bank checksums to those listed in drawing 2021154-. Note that page numbers in the reconstructed code match those on the Artemis 072 printout, although the changed code would likely have changed page numbers for a real Artemis 071 listing.

Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. 

024281,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
024282,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    P20-P25.agc
024283,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     A section of Artemis revision 071.
024284,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the reconstructed source code for the first
024285,000006:                                                                                                  ##              release of the flight software for the Command Module's
024286,000007:                                                                                                  ##              (CM) Apollo Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 15 through
024287,000008:                                                                                                  ##              17. The code has been recreated from a copy of Artemis 072.
024288,000009:                                                                                                  ##              It has been adapted such that the resulting bugger words
024289,000010:                                                                                                  ##              exactly match those specified for Artemis 071 in NASA
024290,000011:                                                                                                  ##              drawing 2021154-, which gives relatively high confidence
024291,000012:                                                                                                  ##              that the reconstruction is correct.
024292,000013:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   552
024293,000014:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL
024294,000015:                                                                                                  ## Contact:     Ron Burkey <info@sandroid.org>.
024295,000016:                                                                                                  ## Website:     www.ibiblio.org/apollo/index.html
024296,000017:                                                                                                  ## Mod history: 2019-08-14 MAS  Created from Artemis 072.
024297,000018:                                                                                                  ##              2021-05-30 ABS  NOUTINPT -> NDUTINPT

024300,000021: 
024301,000022:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
024302,000023:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
024303,000024:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO -1
024304,000025:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - N.BRODEUR
024305,000026: 
024306,000027:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024307,000028: 
024308,000029:                                                                                                  #  TO INITIALIZE THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION SUBROUTINES R22, R61CSM, AND
024309,000030:                                                                                                  #  R52, WHICH IN TURN CONTROL THE CSM ATTITUDE AND OPTICS POSITIONING,
024310,000031:                                                                                                  #  PROCESS BOTH OPTICS AND VHF TRACKING DATA, AND UPDATE EITHER THE LM
024311,000032:                                                                                                  #  OR THE CSM STATE VECTORS.
024312,000033: 
024313,000034:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024314,000035:                                                                                                  #    V37E20E
024315,000036: 
024316,000037:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024317,000038:                                                                                                  #    R22 (RENDEZVOUS TRACK DATA PROCESSING)
024318,000039:                                                                                                  #    R52 (AUTO OPTICS POSITIONING)
024319,000040:                                                                                                  #    R61CSM (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
024320,000041:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH            BANKCALL            UPFLAG
024321,000042:                                                                                                  #    DOWNFLAG           2PHSCHNG            LOADTIME
024322,000043:                                                                                                  #    PRIOCHNG           UPSTATE             INTPRET
024323,000044:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB           MKRLEES             FINDVAC
024324,000045: 
024325,000046:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
024326,000047:                                                                                                  #    RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION MAY BE TERMINATED BY THE SELECTION OF
024327,000048:                                                                                                  #    P00, P06, P22, P23, V34E FROM R60, AND V56E
024328,000049: 
024329,000050:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES
024330,000051:                                                                                                  #    NONE DIRECTLY FROM P20
024331,000052: 
024332,000053:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024333,000054:                                                                                                  #    NONE DIRECTLY FROM P20
024334,000055: 
024335,000056:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
024336,000057:                                                                                                  #    RNDVZFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG, TARG1FLG
024337,000058:                                                                                                  #    PRFTRKAT, V50N18FL
024338,000059: 
024339,000060: 36,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S7                                 
024340,000061: 36,2000                                           BANK                                           
024341,000062: 
024342,000063: 36,2016  E6,1774                                  EBANK=   R61CNTR                               
024343,000064: 36,2016                                           COUNT*   $$/P20                                
024344,000065: 
024345,000066: 36,2016           04636        PROG20             TC       BANKCALL                              
024346,000067: 36,2017           03731                           CADR     R02BOTH                               #  IMU STATUS CHECK
024347,000068:                                                                                                  #  BLOCKING OF UPLINK IS DONE BY UPLINK PRG
024348,000069: 36,2020           31655                           CA       ADB                                   
024349,000070: 36,2021           55773                           TS       DBPTC

025070,000791:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS TRACKING SIGHTING MARK ROUTINE (R21)
025071,000792:                                                                                                  #  AND BACKUP SIGHTING MARK ROUTINE (R23)
025072,000793: 
025073,000794:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
025074,000795:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 1
025075,000796:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - N.BRODEUR
025076,000797:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025077,000798: 
025078,000799:                                                                                                  #    TO PERFORM SIGHTING MARKS IN CONJUNCTION WITH THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIG-
025079,000800:                                                                                                  #  ATION PROGRAM. CALLED BY ASTRONAUT VIA EXTENDED VERB
025080,000801:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
025081,000802:                                                                                                  #          R21 VIA V 57
025082,000803:                                                                                                  #          R23 VIA V 54
025083,000804:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
025084,000805:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
025085,000806:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      GOMARK2         GOMARKF
025086,000807:                                                                                                  #    INTPRET       GENTRAN         KLEENEX
025087,000808:                                                                                                  #    ENDMARK
025088,000809:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
025089,000810:                                                                                                  #    MARKRUPT USED BY SXTMARK HAS BEEN MODIFIED TO STORE MARK IN MRKBUF2
025090,000811:                                                                                                  #  FOR USE BY R22. WHEN ASTRONAUT IS FINISHED TAKING MARKS, HE HITS AN
025091,000812:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED ,   R21 IS TERMINATED THUS CAUSING THE FINAL MARK TO BE TRANSFRD
025092,000813:                                                                                                  #  TO MRKBUF2 FOR PROCESSING BY R22
025093,000814:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
025094,000815:                                                                                                  #    NONE
025095,000816:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
025096,000817:                                                                                                  #    7 REGISTER MRKBUF2 CONTAINING TIME2,TIME1,CDUY,OPTICS X,CDUZ, OPTICS Y,
025097,000818:                                                                                                  #  CDUX.
025098,000819:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025099,000820:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET AND RESET
025100,000821:                                                                                                  #    R21MARK   (COMMUNICATION TO MARKRUPT TO STORE MARKS IN MRKBUF1 + 2)
025101,000822:                                                                                                  #    R23FLG  INDICATES COAS MARKING
025102,000823:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

025263,000984:                                                                                                  #  US,THE MODIFIED FICTITIOUS STAR DIRECTION VECTOR

Page 577 

025344,001065: 
025345,001066:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS TRACKING DATA PROCESSING ROUTINE (R22)
025346,001067: 
025347,001068:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025348,001069: 
025349,001070:                                                                                                  #  TO PROCESS RENDEZVOUS SIGHTING MARK AND VHF RANGING DATA TO UPDATE 
025350,001071:                                                                                                  #  THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER THE CSM OR LM AS DEFINED BY VEHUPFLG.
025351,001072:                                                                                                  #  (VEHUPFLG IS SET TO LM BY P20, CSM BY V81E, AND LM BY V80E.)
025352,001073: 
025353,001074:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
025354,001075:                                                                                                  #    AUTOMATICALLY SELECTED BY P20
025355,001076: 
025356,001077:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025357,001078:                                                                                                  #    PRIOCHNG           INTPRET             GRP2PC
025358,001079:                                                                                                  #    GETUM              BVECTORS            INCORP1
025359,001080:                                                                                                  #    INCORP2            INTEGRV             PHASCHNG
025360,001081:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC              BANKCALL            GOTOV56
025361,001082:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB           INSTALL             DOWNFLAG
025362,001083:                                                                                                  #    TRFAILOF           TRFAILON            TASKOVER
025363,001084:                                                                                                  #    POSTJUMP
025364,001085: 
025365,001086:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
025366,001087:                                                                                                  #    RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION MAY BE TERMINATED BY THE SELECTION OF
025367,001088:                                                                                                  #    P00, P06, P22, P23, V34E FROM R60, AND V56E
025368,001089: 
025369,001090:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS OR ABORT EXIT MODES
025370,001091:                                                                                                  #    NONE
025371,001092: 
025372,001093:                                                                                                  #  INPUT
025373,001094:                                                                                                  #    MARK DATA, SEE R21 AND R23
025374,001095:                                                                                                  #    VHF RANGING DATA
025375,001096: 
025376,001097:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025377,001098:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT, NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS INCORPORATED (COUNTER)
025378,001099:                                                                                                  #    VHFCNT, NO OF VHF RANGING MARKS INCORPORATED (COUNTER)
025379,001100:                                                                                                  #    V06N49, EXCESSIVE UPDATE PARAMETERS-DELTA R AND DELTA V
025380,001101: 
025381,001102:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
025382,001103:                                                                                                  #    SOURCFLG, VINTFLAG, DIM0FLAG, INCORFLG, ORBWFLAG, RENDWFLG
025383,001104:                                                                                                  #    STATEFLG, D6OR9FLG, SKIPVHF, DMENFLG                                 AT THE INTERRUPTED DISPLAY.
025384,001105: 
025385,001106: 34,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S3                                 
025386,001107: 34,2000                                           BANK                                           
025387,001108: 
025388,001109: 34,2625                                           COUNT*   $$/R22

026114,001835:

026116,001837: 04,3302           77754        -DTSCALR           OCT      77754                                 #  -5.9375 MS IN SCALAR
026117,001838: 
026118,001839:                                                                                                  #  CRS61.1       4/10/68
026119,001840:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE CSM WHICH ENABLES

Page 593 

026121,001842:                                                                                                  #  OPTICS TRACKING OF THE LM AND LM TRACKING OF THE CSM RADAR TRANSPONDER
026122,001843:                                                                                                  #  AND TO COMPUTE THE &X-AXIS TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE CSM WHICH ENABLES
026123,001844:                                                                                                  #  COAS TRACKING OF THE LM.
026124,001845:                                                                                                  #    TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE SELECTED TRACKING ATTITUDE IF THE 
026125,001846:                                                                                                  #  MANEUVER IS LESS THAN 10 DEGREES BUT TO CALL R60 IF THE MANEUVER IS
026126,001847:                                                                                                  #  GREATER THAN 10 DEGREES OR IF THE R60FLAG IS SET.
026127,001848:                                                                                                  #           (1) EXTRAPOLATE LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS TO PRESENT TIME USING
026128,001849:                                                                                                  #               CONIC EQUATIONS.
026129,001850: 
026130,001851:                                                                                                  #           (2) CALCULATE LOS FROM CSM TO LM = RL - RC.
026131,001852: 
026132,001853:                                                                                                  #           (3) THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE IS DEFINED AS FOLLOWS:
026133,001854:                                                                                                  #               THE TRACK AXIS (I) IS ALIGNED ALONG THE LOS TO THE LM. THE
026134,001855:                                                                                                  #               TRACK AXIS (I) IS DEFINED AS:
026135,001856: 
026136,001857:                                                                                                  #               UNIT(I)=UNIT(Z  )COS55 &UNIT(X  )SIN55
026137,001858:                                                                                                  #                     -       -SC             -SC
026138,001859:                                                                                                  #           (4) COMPUTE DESIRED CDU ANGLES, USING VECPOINT.
026139,001860:                                                                                                  #           (7) FORM DIFFERENCE BETWEEN DESIRED AND ACTUAL CDUS.
026140,001861:                                                                                                  #               IF ANY OF THE THREE ANGLE DIFFERENCES EXCEEDS 10 DEGREES,
026141,001862:                                                                                                  #               GROSS MANEUVER IS REQUIRED. SIGNAL R61 (SET MPAC=1) TO
026142,001863:                                                                                                  #               OPERATE KALCMANU AND EXIT CRS61.1.
026143,001864:                                                                                                  #               IF ALL DIFFERENCES ARE LESS THAN 10 DEGREES, CONTINUE.
026144,001865: 
026145,001866:                                                                                                  #           (8) CALCULATE ORTHOGONAL LOS RATE IN REF COORDS AS
026146,001867: 
026147,001868:                                                                                                  #               OMEGATH = (UNITLOS(B1) X UNITDV(B1))(ABSDV(B7)/ABSLOS(B29))
026148,001869:                                                                                                  #               CONVERSION FACTOR OF 100/2PI (B4) REV CSEC PER RAD SEC IS
026149,001870:                                                                                                  #               APPLIED TO YIELD UNITS OF REVS/SEC. SCALE IS CARRIED AS
026150,001871:                                                                                                  #               B+1+1+7-29+4+1 PLUS RESULTS OF NORMALIZING ABSDV, ABSLOS.
026151,001872:                                                                                                  #               THE EXTRA B+1 RESULTS FROM RESCALING ABSDV B8 AFTER NORM
026152,001873:                                                                                                  #               TO AVOID OVFLOW ON DIVIDE.
026153,001874: 
026154,001875:                                                                                                  #               UNITLOS = UNIT( RL - RC) B1.
026155,001876:                                                                                                  #               UNITDY  = UNIT( VL - VC) B1.
026156,001877:                                                                                                  #               ABSLOS  = LENGTH OF LOS, METERS B29.
026157,001878:                                                                                                  #               ABSDV   = LENGTH OF DV , METERS/CSEC B7.
026158,001879: 
026159,001880:                                                                                                  #           (9) OBTAIN RATE IN SM COORDS.
026160,001881: 
026161,001882:                                                                                                  #               OMEGATHSM = (REFSMMAT)(OMEGATH).
026162,001883: 
026163,001884:                                                                                                  #           (10)OBTAIN GIMBAL ANGLE INCREMENTS FOR 0.1 SECOND.
026164,001885: 
026165,001886:                                                                                                  #               DTHETASM = (0.1)(OMEGATHSM)
026166,001887: 
026167,001888:                                                                                                  #           (11)OBTAIN DELCDUX,Y,Z USING SUBR SMCDURES.
026168,001889:                                                                                                  #               INPUT CONSISTS OF
026169,001890: 
026170,001891:                                                                                                  #               (A) VECTOR OF ANGULAR INCREMENTS, DTHETASM, STORED

Page 594 

026172,001893:                                                                                                  #                   IN V(DTHETASM).
026173,001894: 
026174,001895:                                                                                                  #               (B) SIN,COS CDUX,Y,Z FROM  SUBR CDUTRIG.
026175,001896: 
026176,001897:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER OUTPUT OF SMCDURES FROM V(DCDU) TO VAC14D.
026177,001898: 
026178,001899:                                                                                                  #           (12)CALCULATE ANG LOS RATE IN BODY(NB) COORDS USING SUBR SMNB.
026179,001900: 
026180,001901:                                                                                                  #               OMEGANB = (SMNB)(OMEGATHSM)
026181,001902: 
026182,001903:                                                                                                  #               SUBR SMNB REQUIRES  OMEGATHSM IN V(VAC32D) AND ACTUAL CDUS
026183,001904:                                                                                                  #               (Y,X,Z ORDER) IN V(VAC20D) WITH S1 OF VAC = BASE ADDRESS
026184,001905:                                                                                                  #               OF CDUS (FIXLOC + 20D).
026185,001906: 
026186,001907:                                                                                                  #           (13)CALCULATE ANG LOS RATE IN CONTROL COORDS AS FOLLOWS
026187,001908: 
026188,001909:                                                                                                  #               WBODY = (MBDYTCTL)(OMEGANB)   UNITS=REVS/SEC(B0).
026189,001910: 
026190,001911:                                                                                                  #                              ( 0.5       0             0      ) BODY TO
026191,001912:                                                                                                  #               MBDYTCTL(B1) = (  0   COS(7.25)B1  -SIN(7.25)B1 )=CONTROL
026192,001913:                                                                                                  #                              (  0   SIN(7.25)B1   COS(7.25)B1 ) AXES
026193,001914:                                                                                                  #                                                                CONVERSION
026194,001915:                                                                                                  #                                                                 MATRIX
026195,001916: 
026196,001917:                                                                                                  #           (14)RESCALE WBODY TO UNITS OF 450 DEG/SEC BY APPLYING FACTOR
026197,001918:                                                                                                  #               OF 0.8 TO REVS/SEC.
026198,001919: 
026199,001920:                                                                                                  #           (15)ADDRESS LIVE AUTOPILOT REGISTERS IN BASIC (UNDER INHINT).
026200,001921: 
026201,001922:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER DESIRED CDUS, SCALED 180 DEGREES, FROM T(SAVEDCDU)
026202,001923:                                                                                                  #               TO V(CDUXD).
026203,001924:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER DELCDUS, SCALED 180 DEG, FROM V(VAC14D)
026204,001925:                                                                                                  #               TO V(DELCDUX).
026205,001926:                                                                                                  #               TRANSFER OMEGA CONTROL, SCALED 450 DEG/SEC, FROM V(MPAC)
026206,001927:                                                                                                  #               TO V(WBODY).
026207,001928:                                                                                                  #               RELINT, SET MPAC=0, EXIT CRS61.1
026208,001929: 
026209,001930:                                                                                                  #  CALL     L  CALL CRS61.1
026210,001931: 
026211,001932:                                                                                                  #  RETURNS  ALL TO L+1.
026212,001933: 
026213,001934:                                                                                                  #           (1) S(MPAC)=0. NORMAL EXIT. 3 SETS OF INPUTS FED TO DAP.
026214,001935:                                                                                                  #           (2) S(MPAC)=1. CALCULATED DESIRED CDUS,SP, SET IN T(CPHI)
026215,001936:                                                                                                  #               FOR KALCMANU. ABS(ACDU - DCDU) EXCEEDS 10 DEGREES.
026216,001937:                                                                                                  #           (3) S(MPAC)=2. GNCS AUTO MODE NOT SELECTED (BIT10=1).
026217,001938:                                                                                                  #           (4) S(MPAC)=3. DAP HOLD FLAG (HOLDFLAG) NOT EQUAL -1.
026218,001939: 
026219,001940:                                                                                                  #  INPUT    (1) TIME2,TIME1. COMPUTER CLOCK TIME,DP, CENTISEC B28.
026220,001941:                                                                                                  #           (2) CDUX,Y,Z. PRESENT CDU ANGLES,SP,2S COMPL HALF-REVS B0.
026221,001942:                                                                                                  #           (3) M(REFSMMAT),STABLE MEMBER COORDS B1.

Page 595 

026223,001944: 
026224,001945:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT   NORMAL. EXIT WITH S(MPAC) = 0.
026225,001946: 
026226,001947:                                                                                                  #           (1) CDUXD,CDUYD,CDUZD, DESIRED OUTER, INNER, MIDDLE CDU ANGLES,
026227,001948:                                                                                                  #               DP, 1S COMPL, SCALED 180 DEGREES (HALF-REVS B0).
026228,001949:                                                                                                  #           (2) DELCDUX,DELCDUY,DELCDUZ. 0.1 SEC DCU ANGULAR INCREMENTS,
026229,001950:                                                                                                  #               DP, 1S COMPL, SCALED 180 DEG.
026230,001951:                                                                                                  #           (3) WBODY,WBODY1,WBODY2. LOS ANGULAR RATE IN CONTROL COORDS,

Page 609 

026877,002598: 
026878,002599:                                                                                                  #  ..... S22.1 ORBITAL NAVIGATION ROUTINE
026879,002600:                                                                                                  #  MOD 1
026880,002601: 
026881,002602:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
026882,002603:                                                                                                  #   1. UPDATE CSM STATE VECTOR
026883,002604:                                                                                                  #   2. UPDATE LANDMARK POSITION
026884,002605:                                                                                                  #   3. CONVERT W MATRIX FROM 9 TO 6 DIMENSIONS
026885,002606: 
026886,002607:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
026887,002608:                                                                                                  #   INTSTALL,INTEGRV,GETUM,SETRE,R-TO-TP,RP-TO-R,BVECTORS,INCORP1,INCORP2
026888,002609:                                                                                                  #   LALOTORV,S22F2410,LAT-LONG,ROWDOT
026889,002610: 
026890,002611:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION
026891,002612:                                                                                                  #   W=9X9 MATRIX
026892,002613:                                                                                                  #   ORBWFLAG=0 FOR INVALID W MATRIX,=1 FOR VALID W MATRIX
026893,002614:                                                                                                  #   ASTRONAUT ENTRY OF KNOWN,L,OFF
026894,002615:                                                                                                  #   8NN= NUMBER OF MARKS  DECIMAL INTEGER B-14
026895,002616:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT= TRANSFORMATION MATRIX
026896,002617:                                                                                                  #   MARKSTAT= ADDRESS OF START OF MARK DATA (MARK DATA OF EACH MARK IS
026897,002618:                                                                                                  #             STORED AS FOLLOWS,  TIME,AIG,SA,AMG,PA,AOG) TIME IS IN DOUBLE
026898,002619:                                                                                                  #             PRECISION,ALL OTHERS ARE IN SINGLE PRECISION
026899,002620:                                                                                                  #   CSM STATE VECTOR
026900,002621: 
026901,002622:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
026902,002623:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED CSM STATE VECTOR
026903,002624:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED LANDMARK POSITION
026904,002625:                                                                                                  #   NEW 6 DIMENSIONAL W MATRIX
026905,002626: 
026906,002627:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
026907,002628:                                                                                                  #   PUSH LIST,CSMPOS,ALPHAV,ERADM,UM,RCLP,USTAR,VARIANCE,X789,BVECTOR,8KK,
026908,002629:                                                                                                  #   S22LOC,SVMRKDAT TABLE,22SUBSCL,LANDMARK,CXOFF,S22C,LAT,LONG,ALT,
026909,002630:                                                                                                  #   TEMPOR1,S22TOFF,S221OFF,DSPTEM1,S22EORM,S22TPRIM
026910,002631: 
026911,002632: 30,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S6                                 
026912,002633: 30,2000                                           BANK                                           
026913,002634: 
026914,002635: 30,2466  E7,1751                                  EBANK=   LANDMARK                              
026915,002636: 30,2466                                           COUNT*   $$/P22

027634,003355: 
027635,003356:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINE NAME:   V89CALL
027636,003357:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO:  0                      DATE: 8 FEB 1968
027637,003358:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY:  DIGITAL DEVEL GROUP    LOG SECTION:  P20-P25
027638,003359: 
027639,003360:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
027640,003361: 
027641,003362:                                                                                                  #  CALLED BY VERB 89 ENTER DURING P00. PRIO 10 USED. CALCULATES AND
027642,003363:                                                                                                  #  DISPLAYS FINAL GIMBAL ANGLES TO POINT CSM +X AXIS OR PREFERRED AXIS
027643,003364:                                                                                                  #  (UNIT(Z)COS55 DEG + UNIT(X)SIN55 DEG) AT LM.
027644,003365: 
027645,003366:                                                                                                  #  1. KEY IN V 89 E ONLY IF IN PROG 00. IF NOT IN P00, OPERATOR ERROR AND
027646,003367:                                                                                                  #  EXIT R63, OTHERWISE CONTINUE.
027647,003368: 
027648,003369:                                                                                                  #  2. IF IN P00, DO IMU STATUS CHECK (R02BOTH). IF IMU ON AND ITS
027649,003370:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION KNOWN TO CGC, CONTINUE.
027650,003371: 
027651,003372:                                                                                                  #  3. FLASH DISPLAY V 04 N 06. R2 INDICATES WHICH SPACECRAFT AXIS IS TO
027652,003373:                                                                                                  #  BE POINTED AT LM.  INITIAL CHOICE IS PREFERRED AXIS. (R2=1).
027653,003374:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT CAN CHANGE TO (+X) AXIS (R2 NOT= 1) BY V22 E 2 E.  CONTINUE
027654,003375:                                                                                                  #  AFTER KEYING IN PROCEED.
027655,003376: 
027656,003377:                                                                                                  #  4. SET PREFERRED ATTITUDE FLAG ACCORDING TO OPTION DESIRED. SET FLAG
027657,003378:                                                                                                  #  FOR PREFERRED AXIS. RESET FLAG FOR X AXIS.
027658,003379: 
027659,003380:                                                                                                  #  5. CURRENT TIME IS STORED AND R63COMP IS CALLED
027660,003381: 
027661,003382:                                                                                                  #      R63COMP JOB:
027662,003383:                                                                                                  #        
027663,003384:                                                                                                  #        UPDATES CSM AND LM STATE VECTORS USING CONIC EQUATIONS
027664,003385: 
027665,003386:                                                                                                  #        CALCULATES BOTH PREFERRED AND X AXIS TRACKING ATT FROM 3SM TO LM.
027666,003387: 
027667,003388:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES AS INDICATED BY PREFERRED ATTITUDE FLAG
027668,003389:                                                                                                  #        ARE STORED FOR LATER R60CSM CALL.
027669,003390: 
027670,003391:                                                                                                  #  6. FLASH DISPLAY V 06 N18 AND AWAIT RESPONSE.
027671,003392: 
027672,003393:                                                                                                  #  7. RECYCLE- RETURN TO STEP 5.
027673,003394:                                                                                                  #     TERMINATE- EXIT R63 ROUTINE
027674,003395:                                                                                                  #     PROCEED- RESET 3AXISFLG AND CALL R60CSM FOR ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
027675,003396: 
027676,003397: 
027677,003398:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: V 89 E
027678,003399: 
027679,003400:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED: CHKPOOH, R02BOTH, GOXDSPF, R63COMP, R60CSM
027680,003401: 
027681,003402:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS   1. OPERATOR ERROR IF NOT IN P00
027682,003403:                                                                                                  #           2. PROGRAM ALARM IF IMU IS OFF
027683,003404:                                                                                                  #           3. PROGRAM ALARM IF IMU ORIENTATION IS UNKNOWN

Page 626 

027685,003406: 
027686,003407:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: NONE
027687,003408: 
027688,003409:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:  OPTION1, OPTION1+1, PRFTRKAT(PREF ATT FLAG),P21TIME, 3AXISFLG

027747,003468: 
027748,003469:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME- P23 CISLUNAR MIDCOURSE NAVIGATION
027749,003470:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO
027750,003471:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY- TOM KNATT
027751,003472:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION- DO MIDCOURSE NAVIGATION BY INCORPORATION OF STAR 
027752,003473:                                                                                                  #  /EARTH AND STAR/MOON OPTICAL MEASUREMENTS.
027753,003474:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE- ASTRONAUT OPERATED
027754,003475:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED-R52,R53,R57,R60,ORBITAL INTEGRATION (INTEGRV)
027755,003476:                                                                                                  #  INCORP1,INCORP2,LALOTORV,LUNPOS  ,AND DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINES.
027756,003477:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES- VIA ROO
027757,003478:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS- NONE
027758,003479:                                                                                                  #  ABORT MODES- NONE
027759,003480:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED- PAD-LOADED ERASABLES,ORBWFLAG RESET,
027760,003481:                                                                                                  #  REFSMFLG=0 IF IMU OFF AND REFSMFLG=1 IF IMU ON
027761,003482:                                                                                                  #  INPUTS BY USER REQUIRED- STAR NUMBER,LANDMARK LAT,LONG/2,ALT
027762,003483:                                                                                                  #  IF LANDMARK IS USED,        NEAR OR FAR HORIZON IF HORIZON IS USED, AND 
027763,003484:                                                                                                  #  BODY TO BE MARKED ON (EARTH OR MOON).  SEE GSOP CHAPT 4.
027764,003485:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-UPDATED CMC STATE VECTOR. VECTOR FROM S/C TO HORIZON OR LANDMARK
027765,003486:                                                                                                  #  IN POINTAXS. POINTAXS CAN BE USED TO GENERATE THIS VECTOR APART FROM
027766,003487:                                                                                                  #  P23 IF DESIRED.
027767,003488:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS-NO USABLE DEBRIS IS GENERATED. RENDWFLG IS RESET FOR P20 UPON
027768,003489:                                                                                                  #  ENTRY INTO P23.    RUPTREGS AND ERASABLES USED BY DISPLAYS ARE DEBRIS
